	focus = {
		id = GER_demand_slovenia
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_anschluss }
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_political_pressure
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = GER_fate_of_yugoslavia }
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			controls_state = 16
		}
		allow_branch = {
			always = no
		}
		will_lead_to_war_with = YUG
		bypass = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					YUG = { owns_state = 102 }
				}
				has_war_with = YUG
				is_in_faction_with = YUG
				YUG = { is_subject_of = GER }
			}
		}
		cancel_if_invalid = yes
		x = 2
		y = 2
		relative_position_id = GER_anschluss
		cost = 2
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}	
		completion_reward = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = YUG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = GER_fate_of_yugoslavia
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_anschluss }

		available = {
			is_puppet = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = YUG }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = YUG }
			date > 1941.1.1

			always = no

		bypass = {
			OR = {

						is_puppet_of = PREV

	##### TRIPARTITE #####
	
	focus = {
		id = GER_japan_friend
		icon = GFX_GER_japan_friend
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = NO_ASIA

				}
				AND = {
					JAP = { is_puppet = no }
					NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
				}
			}
			else = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = JAP
				JAP = { is_puppet = no }
				NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
			}
		}
		}
		x = -5
		y = 0
		cost = 2

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			JAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = ger_jap_diplomacy_focus }
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = withdrew_advisors }
				country_event = { id = china.3 hours = 6 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_japan_friend_tt
			set_global_flag = falkenhausen_recalled
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
				}
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Alexander von Falkenhausen"
					gfx = GFX_portrait_chi_alexander_von_falkenhausen
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 3
					logistics_skill = 3
					id = 603
					traits = { infantry_officer }
				}
			}
		}
	}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = NO_ASIA

				}
				AND = {
					JAP = { is_puppet = no }
					NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
				}
			}
			else = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = JAP
					JAP = { is_puppet = no }
					NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
				}
			}
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_japan_friend }
		x = 0
		y = 1
		cost = 2
		relative_position_id = GER_japan_friend

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			add_ideas = GER_JAP_trade
			JAP = { add_ideas = JAP_GER_trade }
		}
	}
	
	focus = {
		id = GER_italy_friend
		icon = GFX_focus_chi_reach_out_to_italy
		available = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = ITA
				ITA = { is_puppet = no }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
			}
		}
		x = -3
		y = 0
		cost = 2
		

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			ITA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = ger_jap_diplomacy_focus }
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 2 }
			ITA = { add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 2 } }
			ITA = { add_offsite_building = { type = dockyard level = 2 } }
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = GER_italy_friend2
		icon = GFX_ger_alliance_with_italy
		available = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = ITA
				ITA = { is_puppet = no }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
			}
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_italy_friend }
		x = 0
		y = 1
		cost = 2
		relative_position_id = GER_italy_friend
		

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			add_ideas = GER_ITA_trade
			ITA= { add_ideas = ITA_GER_trade }
			ITA = { add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 2 } }
		}
	}
	
	focus = {
		id = GER_tripartite
		icon = GFX_goal_indyclone_the_axis
		available = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = ITA
				ITA = { is_puppet = no }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
			}
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_japan_friend2 }
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_italy_friend2 }
		x = -1
		y = 1
		cost = 2
		relative_position_id = GER_italy_friend2
		

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			# ITA = { give_guarantee = GER }
			# JAP = { give_guarantee = GER }
			# JAP = { give_guarantee = ITA }
			# ITA = { give_guarantee = JAP }
			# give_guarantee = JAP
			# give_guarantee = ITA
			
			GER = {
				add_ideas = GER_axis_research_group
			}
			ITA= {
				add_ideas = ITA_axis_research_group
			}
			JAP = {
				add_ideas = JAP_axis_research_group
			}
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = GER_trip_research
			ITA = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = GER_trip_research }
			JAP = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = GER_trip_research }
		}
	}
